{len(analysis_result.get(\'foreshadows\', []))}个")\n146\t                    logger.info(f"  - 情节点: {len(analysis_result.get(\'plot_points\', []))}个")\n147\t                    logger.info(f"  - 整体评分: {analysis_result.get(\'scores\', {}).get(\'overall\', \'N/A\')}")\n148\t                    return analysis_result\n149\t                else:\n150\t                    # JSON解析失败，重试\n151\t                    logger.warning(f"⚠️ JSON解析失败, 尝试 {attempt}/{max_retries}")\n152\t                    last_error = "JSON解析失败"\n153\t                    if attempt < max_retries:\n154\t                        wait_time = min(2 ** attempt, 10)\n155\t                        logger.info(f"  ⏳ 等待 {wait_time} 秒后重试...")\n156\t                        # 调用重试回调，通知调用方正在重试\n157\t                        if on_retry:\n158\t                            try:\n159\t                                await on_retry(attempt, max_retries, wait_time, last_error)\n160\t                            except Exception as callback_error:\n161\t                                logger.warning(f"⚠️ 重试回调执行失败: {callback_error}")\n162\t                        await asyncio.sleep(wait_time)\n163\t                        continue\n164\t                    else:\n165\t                        logger.error(f"❌ 第{chapter_number}章分析失败: JSON解析错误，已达最大重试次数")\n166\t                        return None\n167\t                    \n168\t            except Exception as e:\n169\t                last_error = str(e)\n170\t                logger.error(f"❌ 章节分析异常(尝试 {attempt}/{max_retries}): {last_error}")\n171\t                \n172\t                if attempt < max_retries:\n173\t                    wait_time = min(2 ** attempt, 10)\n174\t                    logger.info(f"  ⏳ 等待 {wait_time} 秒后重试...")\n175\t                    # 调用重试回调，通知调用方正在重试\n176\t                    if on_retry:\n177\t                        try:\n178\t                            await on_retry(attempt, max_retries, wait_time, last_error)\n179\t                        except Exception as callback_error:\n180\t                            logger.warning(f"⚠️ 重试回调执行失败: {callback_error}")\n181\t                    await asyncio.sleep(wait_time)\n182\t                    continue\n183\t                else:\n184\t                    logger.error(f"❌ 第{chapter_number}章分析失败: {last_error}，已达最大重试次数")\n185\t                    return None\n186\t        \n187\t        # 不应该到达这里，但作为安全措施\n188\t        logger.error(f"❌ 第{chapter_number}章分析失败: {last_error}")\n189\t        return None\n190\t    \n191\t    def _format_existing_foreshadows(self, foreshadows: Optional[List[Dict[str, Any]]]) -> str:\n192\t        """\n193\t        格式化已有伏笔列表，用于注入到分析提示词中\n194\t        \n195\t        核心策略（重构版）：\n196\t        - 分层展示所有已埋入伏笔，让AI能识别"自然回收"\n197\t        - 第1层：本章必须回收的伏笔（最详细）\n198\t        - 第2层：超期伏笔（较详细）\n199\t        - 第3层：其他已埋入伏笔（精简信息，供AI判断是否自然回收了）\n200\t        \n201\t        Args:\n202\t            foreshadows: 伏笔列表，每个包含 id, title, content, plant_chapter_number, resolve_status 等\n203\t        \n204\t        Returns:\n205\t            格式化的文本\n206\t        """\n207\t        if not foreshadows:\n208\t            return "（暂无已埋入的伏笔）"\n209\t        \n210\t        # 分类伏笔\n211\t        must_resolve = [fs for fs in foreshadows if fs.get(\'resolve_status\') == \'must_resolve_now\']\n212\t        overdue = [fs for fs in foreshadows if fs.get(\'resolve_status\') == \'overdue\']\n213\t        others = [fs for fs in foreshadows if fs.get(\'resolve_status\') not in (\'must_resolve_now\', \'overdue\')]\n214\t        \n215\t        lines = []\n216\t        \n217\t        # === 第1层：本章必须回收的伏笔（最详细）===\n218\t        if must_resolve:\n219\t            lines.append("=" * 40)\n220\t            lines.append("【🎯 本章必须回收的伏笔】")\n221\t            lines.append("=" * 40)\n222\t            for i, fs in enumerate(must_resolve, 1):\n223\t                fs_id = fs.get(\'id\', \'unknown\')\n224\t                fs_title = fs.get(\'title\', \'未命名伏笔\')\n225\t                fs_content = fs.get(\'content\', \'\')[:200]\n226\t                plant_chapter = fs.get(\'plant_chapter_number\', \'?\')\n227\t                hint_text = fs.get(\'hint_text\', \'\')\n228\t                \n229\t                lines.append(f"{i}. 【ID: {fs_id}】{fs_title}")\n230\t                lines.append(f"   埋入章节：第{plant_chapter}章")\n231\t                lines.append(f"   伏笔内容：{fs_content}{\'...\' if len(fs.get(\'content\', \'\')) > 200 else \'\'}")\n232\t                if hint_text:\n233\t                    lines.append(f"   埋入暗示：{hint_text[:100]}")\n234\t                lines.append(f"   ⚠️ 回收时 reference_foreshadow_id 填写: {fs_id}")\n235\t                lines.append("")\n236\t        \n237\t        # === 第2层：超期伏笔 ===\n238\t        if overdue:\n239\t            lines.append("【⚠️ 超期未回收伏笔 - 如章节内容回收了请标记】")\n240\t            for fs in overdue[:5]:\n241\t                fs_id = fs.get(\'id\', \'unknown\')\n242\t                fs_title = fs.get(\'title\', \'\')\n243\t                plant_chapter = fs.get(\'plant_chapter_number\', \'?\')\n244\t                lines.append(f"- 【ID: {fs_id}】{fs_title}（第{plant_chapter}章埋入）")\n245\t            lines.append("")\n246\t        \n247\t        # === 第3层：其他已埋入伏笔（精简）===\n248\t        if others:\n249\t            lines.append("【📋 其他已埋入伏笔 - 如章节内容自然回收了请标记】")\n250\t            for fs in others[:10]:\n251\t                fs_id = fs.get(\'id\', \'unknown\')\n252\t                fs_title = fs.get(\'title\', \'\')\n253\t                plant_chapter = fs.get(\'plant_chapter_number\', \'?\')\n254\t                lines.append(f"- 【ID: {fs_id}】{fs_title}（第{plant_chapter}章埋入）")\n255\t            if len(others) > 10:\n256\t                lines.append(f"  ... 还有{len(others) - 10}个伏笔未列出")\n257\t            lines.append("")\n258\t        \n259\t        # 操作指引\n260\t        lines.append("提示：如果章节内容回收了上述任一伏笔，请在 foreshadows 数组中")\n261\t        lines.append("添加 type=\'resolved\' 的记录，并在 reference_foreshadow_id 填写对应ID。")\n262\t        \n263\t        return "\\n".join(lines)\n264\t    \n265\t    def _parse_analysis_response(self, response: str) -> Optional[Dict[str, Any]]:\n266\t        """\n267\t        解析AI返回的分析结果（使用统一的JSON清洗方法）\n268\t        \n269\t        Args:\n270\t            response: AI返回的文本\n271\t        \n272\t        Returns:\n273\t            解析后的字典,失败返回None\n274\t        """\n275\t        try:\n276\t            # 使用统一的JSON清洗方法\n277\t            cleaned = self.ai_service._clean_json_response(response)\n278\t            \n279\t            # 尝试解析JSON\n280\t            result = json.loads(cleaned)\n281\t            \n282\t            # 验证必要字段\n283\t            required_fields = [\'hooks\', \'plot_points\', \'scores\']\n284\t            for field in required_fields:\n285\t                if field not in result:\n286\t                    logger.warning(f"⚠️ 分析结果缺少字段: {field}")\n287\t                    result[field] = [] if field != \'scores\' else {}\n288\t            \n289\t            logger.info("✅ 成功解析分析结果")\n290\t            return result\n291\t            \n292\t        except json.JSONDecodeError as e:\n293\t            logger.error(f"❌ JSON解析失败: {str(e)}")\n294\t            logger.error(f"  原始响应(前500字): {response[:500]}")\n295\t            return None\n296\t        except Exception as e:\n297\t            logger.error(f"❌ 解析异常: {str(e)}")\n298\t            return None\n299\t    \n300\t    def extract_memories_from_analysis(\n301\t        self,\n302\t        analysis: Dict[str, Any],\n303\t        chapter_id: str,\n304\t        chapter_number: int,\n305\t        chapter_content: str = "",\n306\t        chapter_title: str = ""\n307\t    ) -> List[Dict[str, Any]]:\n308\t        """\n309\t        从分析结果中提取记忆片段\n310\t        \n311\t        Args:\n312\t            analysis: 分析结果\n313\t            chapter_id: 章节ID\n314\t            chapter_number: 章节号\n315\t            chapter_content: 章节完整内容(用于计算位置)\n316\t            chapter_title: 章节标题\n317\t        \n318\t        Returns:\n319\t            记忆片段列表\n320\t        """\n321\t        memories = []\n322\t        \n323\t        try:\n324\t            # 【新增】0. 提取章节摘要作为记忆（用于语义检索相关章节）\n325\t            chapter_summary = ""\n326\t            \n327\t            # 尝试从分析结果获取摘要\n328\t            if analysis.get(\'summary\'):\n329\t                chapter_summary = analysis.get(\'summary\')\n330\t            # 或者从情节点组合生成摘要\n331\t            elif analysis.get(\'plot_points\'):\n332\t                plot_summaries = [p.get(\'content\', \'\') for p in analysis.get(\'plot_points\', [])[:3]]\n333\t                chapter_summary = "；".join(plot_summaries)\n334\t            # 或者使用内容前300字\n335\t            elif chapter_content:\n336\t                chapter_summary = chapter_content[:300] + ("..." if len(chapter_content) > 300 else "")\n337\t            \n338\t            # 如果有摘要，添加到记忆中\n339\t            if chapter_summary:\n340\t                memories.append({\n341\t                    \'type\': \'chapter_summary\',\n342\t                    \'content\': chapter_summary,\n343\t                    \'title\': f"第{chapter_number}章《{chapter_title}》摘要",\n344\t                    \'metadata\': {\n345\t                        \'chapter_id\': chapter_id,\n346\t                        \'chapter_number\': chapter_number,\n347\t                        \'importance_score\': 0.6,  # 中等重要性\n348\t                        \'tags\': [\'摘要\', \'章节概览\', chapter_title],\n349\t                        \'is_foreshadow\': 0,\n350\t                        \'text_position\': 0,\n351\t                        \'text_length\': len(chapter_summary)\n352\t                    }\n353\t                })\n354\t                logger.info(f"  ✅ 添加章节摘要记忆: {len(chapter_summary)}字")\n355\t            \n356\t            # 1. 提取钩子作为记忆\n357\t            for i, hook in enumerate(analysis.get(\'hooks\', [])):\n358\t                if hook.get(\'strength\', 0) >= 6:  # 只保存强度>=6的钩子\n359\t                    keyword =             \'content\': f"[{hook.get(\'type\', \'未知\')}钩子] {hook.get(\'content\', \'\')}",\n367\t                        \'title\': f"{hook.get(\'type\', \'钩子\')} - {hook.get(\'position\', \'\')}",\n368\t                        \'metadata\': {\n369\t                            \'chapter_id\': chapter_id,\n370\t                            \'chapter_number\': chapter_number,\n371\t                            \'importance_score\': min(hook.get(\'strength\', 5) / 10, 1.0),\n372\t                            \'tags\': [hook.get(\'type\', \'钩子\'), hook.get(\'position\', \'\')],\n373\t                            \'is_foreshadow\': 0,\n374\t                            \'keyword\': keyword,\n375\t                            \'text_position\': position,\n376\t                            \'text_length\': length,\n377\t                            \'strength\': hook.get(\'strength\', 5),\n378\t                            \'position_desc\': hook.get(\'position\', \'\')\n379\t                        }\n380\t                    })\n381\t            \n382\t            # 2. 提取伏笔作为记忆\n383\t            for i, foreshadow in enumerate(analysis.get(\'foreshadows\', [])):\n384\t                is_planted = foreshadow.get(\'type\') == \'planted\'\n385\t                keyword = foreshadow.get(\'keyword\', \'\')\n386\t                position, length = self._find_text_position(chapter_content, keyword)\n387\t                \n388\t                logger.info(f"  伏笔位置: keyword=\'{keyword[:30]}...\', pos={position}, len={length}")\n389\t                \n390\t                memories.append({\n391\t                    \'type\': \'foreshadow\',\n392\t                    \'content\': foreshadow.get(\'content\', \'\'),\n393\t                    \'title\': f"{\'埋下伏笔\' if is_planted else \'回收伏笔\'}",\n394\t                    \'metadata\': {\n395\t                        \'chapter_id\': chapter_id,\n396\t                        \'chapter_number\': chapter_number,\n397\t                        \'importance_score\': min(foreshadow.get(\'strength\', 5) / 10, 1.0),\n398\t                        \'tags\': [\'伏笔\', foreshadow.get(\'type\', \'planted\')],\n399\t                        \'is_foreshadow\': 1 if is_planted else 2,\n400\t                        \'reference_chapter\': foreshadow.get(\'reference_chapter\'),\n401\t                        \'keyword\': keyword,\n402\t                        \'text_position\': position,\n403\t                        \'text_length\': length,\n404\t                        \'foreshadow_type\': foreshadow.get(\'type\', \'planted\'),\n405\t                        \'strength\': foreshadow.get(\'strength\', 5)\n406\t                    }\n407\t                })\n408\t            \n409\t            # 3. 提取关键情节点\n410\t            for i, plot_point in enumerate(analysis.get(\'plot_points\', [])):\n411\t                if plot_point.get(\'importance\', 0) >= 0.6:  # 只保存重要性>=0.6的情节点\n412\t                    keyword = plot_point.get(\'keyword\', \'\')\n413\t                    position, length = self._find_text_position(chapter_content, keyword)\n414\t                    \n415\t                    logger.info(f"  情节点位置: keyword=\'{keyword[:30]}...\', pos={position}, len={length}")\n416\t                    \n417\t                    memories.append({\n418\t                        \'type\': \'plot_point\',\n419\t                        \'content\': f"{plot_point.get(\'content\', \'\')}。影响: {plot_point.get(\'impact\', \'\')}",\n420\t                        \'title\': f"情节点 - {plot_point.get(\'type\', \'未知\')}",\n421\t                        \'metadata\': {\n422\t                            \'chapter_id\': chapter_id,\n423\t                            \'chapter_number\': chapter_number,\n424\t                            \'importance_score\': plot_point.get(\'importance\', 0.5),\n425\t                            \'tags\': [\'情节点\', plot_point.get(\'type\', \'未知\')],\n426\t                            \'is_foreshadow\': 0,\n427\t                            \'keyword\': keyword,\n428\t                            \'text_position\': position,\n429\t                            \'text_length\': length\n430\t                        }\n431\t                    })\n432\t            \n433\t            # 4. 提取角色状态变化\n434\t            for i, char_state in enumerate(analysis.get(\'character_states\', [])):\n435\t                char_name = char_state.get(\'character_name\', \'未知角色\')\n436\t                memories.append({\n437\t                    \'type\': \'character_event\',\n438\t                    \'content\': f"{char_name}的状态变化: {char_state.get(\'state_before\', \'\')} → {char_state.get(\'state_after\', \'\')}。{char_state.get(\'psychological_change\', \'\')}",\n439\t                    \'title\': f"{char_name}的变化",\n440\t                    \'metadata\': {\n441\t                        \'chapter_id\': chapter_id,\n442\t                        \'chapter_number\': chapter_number,\n443\t                        \'importance_score\': 0.7,\n444\t                        \'tags\': [\'角色\', char_name, \'状态变化\'],\n445\t                        \'related_characters\': [char_name],\n446\t                        \'is_foreshadow\': 0\n447\t                    }\n448\t                })\n449\t            \n450\t            # 5. 如果有重要冲突,也记录下来\n451\t            conflict = analysis.get(\'conflict\', {})\n452\t            \n453\t            if conflict and conflict.get(\'level\', 0) >= 7:\n454\t                # 确保 parties 和 types 都是字符串列表\n455\t                parties = conflict.get(\'parties\', [])\n456\t                if parties and isinstance(parties, list):\n457\t                    parties = [str(p) for p in parties]\n458\t                \n459\t                types = conflict.get(\'types\', [])\n460\t                if types and isinstance(types, list):\n461\t                    types = [str(t) for t in types]\n462\t                \n463\t                memories.append({\n464\t                    \'type\': \'plot_point\',\n465\t                    \'content\': f"重要冲突: {conflict.get(\'description\', \'\')}。冲突各方: {\', \'.join(parties)}",\n466\t                    \'title\': f"冲突 - 强度{conflict.get(\'level\', 0)}",\n467\t                    \'metadata\': {\n468\t                        \'chapter_id\': chapter_id,\n469\t                        \'chapter_number\': \'is_foreshadow\': 0\n473\t                    }\n474\t                })\n475\t            \n476\t            logger.info(f"📝 从分析中提取了{len(memories)}条记忆")\n477\t            return memories\n478\t            \n479\t        except Exception as e:\n480\t            logger.error(f"❌ 提取记忆失败: {str(e)}")\n481\t            return []\n482\t    \n483\t    def _find_text_position(self, full_text: str, keyword: str) -> tuple[int, int]:\n484\t        """\n485\t        在全文中查找关键词位置\n486\t        \n487\t        Args:\n488\t            full_text: 完整文本\n489\t            keyword: 关键词\n490\t        \n491\t        Returns:\n492\t            (起始位置, 长度) 如果未找到返回(-1, 0)\n493\t        """\n494\t        if not keyword or not full_text:\n495\t            return (-1, 0)\n496\t        \n497\t        try:\n498\t            # 1. 精确匹配\n499\t            pos = full_text.find(keyword)\n500\t            if pos != -1:\n501\t                return (pos, len(keyword))\n502\t            \n503\t            # 2. 去除标点符号后匹配\n504\t            import re\n505\t            clean_keyword = re.sub(r\'[，。！？、；：""\'\'（）《》【】]\', \'\', keyword)\n506\t            clean_text = re.sub(r\'[，。！？、；：""\'\'（）《》【】]\', \'\', full_text)\n507\t            pos = clean_text.find(clean_keyword)\n508\t            \n509\t            if pos != -1:\n510\t                # 反向映射到原文位置（简化处理）\n511\t                return (pos, len(clean_keyword))\n512\t            \n513\t            # 3. 模糊匹配：查找关键词的前半部分\n514\t            if len(keyword) > 10:\n515\t                partial = keyword[:min(15, len(keyword))]\n516\t                pos = full_text.find(partial)\n517\t                if pos != -1:\n518\t                    return (pos, len(partial))\n519\t            \n520\t            # 4. 未找到\n521\t            logger.debug(f"未找到关键词位置: {keyword[:30]}...")\n522\t            return (-1, 0)\n523\t            \n524\t        except Exception as e:\n525\t            logger.error(f"查找位置失败: {str(e)}")\n526\t            return (-1, 0)\n527\t    \n528\t    def generate_analysis_summary(self, analysis: Dict[str, Any]) -> str:\n529\t        """\n530\t        生成分析摘要文本\n531\t        \n532\t        Args:\n533\t            analysis: 分析结果\n534\t        \n535\t        Returns:\n536\t            格式化的摘要文本\n537\t        """\n538\t        try:\n539\t            lines = ["=== 章节分析报告 ===\\n"]\n540\t            \n541\t            # 整体评分\n542\t            scores = analysis.get(\'scores\', {})\n543\t            lines.append(f"【整体评分】")\n544\t            lines.append(f"  整体质量: {scores.get(\'overall\', \'N/A\')}/10")\n545\t            lines.append(f"  节奏把控: {scores.get(\'pacing\', \'N/A\')}/10")\n546\t            lines.append(f"  吸引力: {scores.get(\'engagement\', \'N/A\')}/10")\n547\t            lines.append(f"  连贯性: {scores.get(\'coherence\', \'N/A\')}/10\\n")\n548\t            \n549\t            # 剧情阶段\n550\t            lines.append(f"【剧情阶段】{analysis.get(\'plot_stage\', \'未知\')}\\n")\n551\t            \n552\t            # 钩子统计\n553\t            hooks = analysis.get(\'hooks\', [])\n554\t            if hooks:\n555\t                lines.append(f"【钩子分析】共{len(hooks)}个")\n556\t                for hook in hooks[:3]:  # 只显示前3个\n557\t                    lines.append(f"  • [{hook.get(\'type\')}] {hook.get(\'content\', \'\')[:50]}... (强度:{hook.get(\'strength\', 0)})")\n558\t                lines.append("")\n559\t            \n560\t            # 伏笔统计\n561\t            foreshadows = analysis.get(\'foreshadows\', [])\n562\t            if foreshadows:\n563\t                planted = sum(1 for f in foreshadows if f.get(\'type\') == \'planted\')\n564\t                resolved = sum(1 for f in foreshadows if f.get(\'type\') == \'resolved\')\n565\t                lines.append(f"【伏笔分析】埋下{planted}个, 回收{resolved}个\\n")\n566\t            \n567\t            # 冲突分析\n568\t            conflict = analysis.get(\'conflict\', {})\n569\t            if conflict:\n570\t                lines.append(f"【冲突分析】")\n571\t                lines.append(f"  类型: {\', \'.join(conflict.get(\'types\', []))}")\n572\t                lines.append(f"  强度: {conflict.get(\'level\', 0)}/10")\n573\t                lines.append(f"  进度: {int(conflict.get(\'resolution_progress\', 0) * 100)}%\\n")\n574\t            \n575\t            # 改进建议\n576\t            suggestions = analysis.get(\'suggestions\', [])\n577\t            if suggestions:\n578\t                lines.append(f"【改进建议】")\n579\t                for i, sug in enumerate(suggestions, 1):\n580\t                    lines.append(f"  {i}. {sug}")\n581\t            \n582\t            return "\\n".join(lines)\n583\t            \n584\t        except Exception as e:\n585\t            logger.error(f"❌ 生成摘要失败: {str(e)}")\n586\t            return "分析摘要生成失败"\n587\t\n588\t\n589\t# 创建全局实例(需要时手动初始化)\n590\t_plot_analyzer_instance = None\n591\t\n592\tdef get_plot_analyzer(ai_service: AIService) -> PlotAnalyzer:\n593\t    """获取剧情分析器实例"""\n594\t    global _plot_analyzer_instance\n595\t    if _plot_analyzer_instance is None:\n596\t        _plot_analyzer_instance = PlotAnalyzer(ai_service)\n597\t    return _plot_analyzer_instance'}]

generate_stable_foreshadow_id(chapter_id: str, content: str, foreshadow_type: str = "planted") -> str:\n25\t    """\n26\t    生成稳定的伏笔唯一标识符\n27\t    \n28\t    使用 chapter_id + content_hash 的方式，确保：\n29\t    1. 同一章节、相同内容的伏笔只有一个唯一ID\n30\t    2. 重新分析同一章节不会产生新ID\n31\t    3. 标识符足够短且可读\n32\t    \n33\t    Args:\n34\t        chapter_id: 章节ID\n35\t        content: 伏笔内容\n36\t        foreshadow_type: 伏笔类型（planted/resolved）\n37\t    \n38\t    Returns:\n39\t        稳定的唯一标识符，格式：{type}_{chapter_id_hash}_{content_hash}\n40\t    """\n41\t    # 生成内容哈希（取前12位，足够区分）\n42\t    content_normalized = content.strip().lower()\n43\t    content_hash = hashlib.md5(content_normalized.encode(\'utf-8\')).hexdigest()[:12]\n44\t    \n45\t    # 生成章节ID哈希（取前8位）\n46\t    chapter_hash =          data: 同步请求数据\n501\t        \n502\t        Returns:\n503\t            同步结果\n504\t        """\n505\t        try:\n506\t            total_stats = {\n507\t                "synced_count": 0,\n508\t                "skipped_count": 0,\n509\t                "resolved_count": 0,\n510\t                "new_foreshadows": [],\n511\t                "skipped_reasons": []\n512\t            }\n513\t            \n514\t            # 获取分析结果\n515\t            query = select(PlotAnalysis).where(PlotAnalysis.project_id == project_id)\n516\t            if data.chapter_ids:\n517\t                query = query.where(PlotAnalysis.chapter_id.in_(data.chapter_ids))\n518\t            \n519\t            result = await db.execute(query)\n520\t            analyses = result.scalars().all()\n521\t            \n522\t            for analysis in analyses:\n523\t                if not analysis.foreshadows:\n524\t                    continue\n525\t                \n526\t                # 获取章节信息\n527\t                chapter_result = await db.execute(\n528\t                    select(Chapter).where(Chapter.id == analysis.chapter_id)\n529\t                )\n530\t                chapter = chapter_result.scalar_one_or_none()\n531\t                if not chapter:\n532\t                    continue\n533\t                \n534\t                # 委托给统一的处理方法\n535\t                chapter_stats = await self.auto_update_from_analysis(\n536\t                    db=db,\n537\t                    project_id=project_id,\n538\t                    chapter_id=chapter.id,\n539\t                    chapter_number=chapter.chapter_number,\n540\t                    analysis_foreshadows=analysis.foreshadows\n541\t                )\n542\t                \n543\t                # 汇总统计\n544\t                total_stats["synced_count"] += chapter_stats.get("planted_count", 0) + chapter_stats.get("resolved_count", 0)\n545\t                total_stats["resolved_count"] += chapter_stats.get("resolved_count", 0)\n546\t                total_stats["skipped_count"] += chapter_stats.get("skipped_resolve_count", 0)\n547\t            \n548\t            logger.info(f"✅ 伏笔同步完成: 同步{total_stats[\'synced_count\']}个（其中回收{total_stats[\'resolved_count\']}个）, 跳过{total_stats[\'skipped_count\']}个")\n549\t            \n550\t            return total_stats\n551\t            \n552\t        except Exception as e:\n553\t            await db.rollback()\n554\t            logger.error(f"❌ 同步伏笔失败: {str(e)}")\n555\t            raise\n556\t    \n557\t    async def get_pending_resolve_foreshadows(\n558\t        self,\n559\t        db: AsyncSession,\n560\t        project_id: str,\n561\t        current_chapter: int,\n562\t        lookahead: int = 5\n563\t    ) -> 当前章节号\n571\t            lookahead: 向前看几章\n572\t        \n573\t        Returns:\n574\t            待回收伏笔列表\n575\t        """\n576\t        try:\n577\t            # 查询已埋入且计划在接下来几章回收的伏笔\n578\t          Foreshadow.status == "planted",\n584\t                        Foreshadow.target_resolve_chapter_number != None,\n585\t                        Foreshadow.target_resolve_chapter_number <= .order_by(Foreshadow.target_resolve_chapter_number)\n590\t            )\n591\t            \n592\t            result = await db.execute(query)\n593\t            return get_must_resolve_foreshadows(\n638\t        self,\n639\t        db: AsyncSession,\n640\t        project_id: str,\n641\t        chapter_number: int\n642\t    ) -> List[Foreshadow]:\n643\t        """\n644\t        获取本章必须回收的伏笔（target_resolve_chapter_number == chapter_number）\n645\t        \n646\t        这些伏笔是用户明确指定在本章回收的，必须在本章完成回收\n647\t        \n648\t        Args:\n649\t            db: 数据库会话\n650\t            project_id: 项目ID\n651\t            chapter_number: 当前章节号\n652\t        \n653\t        Returns:\n654\t            必须回收的伏笔列表\n655\t        """\n656\t        try:\n657\t           Foreshadow.status == "planted",\n663\t                        Foreshadow.target_resolve_chapter_number == chapter_number\n664\t                    )\n665\t                )\n666\t                .order_by(desc(Foreshadow.importance))\n667\t            )\n668\t            \n669\t            result = await db.execute(query)\n670\t            return list(result.scalars().all())\n671\t            \n672\t        except Exception as e:\n673\t            logger.error(f"❌ 获取本章必须回收伏笔失败: {str(e)}")\n674\t            return []\n675\t    \n676\t    async def get_foreshadows_to_plant(\n677\t        self,\n678\t        db: AsyncSession,\n679\t        project_id: str,\n680\t        chapter_number: int\n681\t    ) -> List[Foreshadow]:\n682\t        """\n683\t        获取计划在本章埋入的伏笔\n684\t        \n685\t        Args:\n686\t            db: 数据库会话\n687\t            project_id: 项目ID\n688\t            chapter_number: 章节号\n689\t        \n690\t        Returns:\n691\t            待埋入伏笔列表\n692\t     )\n702\t                )\n703\t                .order_by(desc(Foreshadow.importance))\n704\t            )\n705\t            \n706\t            result = await db.execute(query)\n707\t async def build_chapter_context(\n714\t        self,\n715\t        db: AsyncSession,\n716\t        project_id: str,\n717\t        chapter_number: int,\n718\t        include_pending: bool = True,\n719\t        include_overdue: bool = True,\n720\t        lookahead: int = 5\n721\t    ) -> Dict[str, Any]:\n722\t        """\n723\t        构建章节生成的伏笔上下文（智能分层提醒策略）\n724\t        \n725\t        核心策略：\n726\t        1. 本章必须回收的伏笔 → 明确要求回收\n727\t        2. 超期伏笔 → 强调需要尽快回收\n728\t        3. 即将回收的伏笔 → 仅作为背景信息，明确禁止提前回收\n729\t        4. 远期伏笔 → 不发送，防止干扰\n730\t        \n731\t        Args:\n732\t            db: 数据库会话\n733\t            project_id: 项目ID\n734\t            chapter_number: 章节号\n735\t            include_pending: 包含待埋入伏笔\n736\t            include_overdue: 包含超期伏笔\n737\t            lookahead: 向前看几章（用于背景提醒，非强制回收）\n738\t        \n739\t        Returns:\n740\t            伏笔上下文信息\n741\t        """\n742\t        try:\n743\t            lines = []\n744\t            to_plant = []\n745\t            must_resolve = []  # 本章必须回收\n746\t            overdue = []       # 超期待回收\n747\t            upcoming = []      # 即将回收（仅参考）\n748\t            \n749\t            # 1. 获取本章必须回收的伏笔（target_resolve_chapter_number == chapter_number）\n750\t            must_resolve = await self.get_must_resolve_foreshadows(db, project_id, chapter_number)\n751\t            if must_resolve:\n752\t                lines.append("【🎯 本章必须回收的伏笔 - 请务必在本章完成回收】")\n753\t                for f in must_resolve:\n754\t                    lines.append(f"- ID:{f.id[:8]} | {f.title}")\n755\t                    lines.append(f"  埋入章节：第{f.plant_chapter_number}章")\n756\t                    lines.append(f"  伏笔内容：{f.content[:100]}{\'...\' if len(f.content) > 100 else \'\'}")\n757\t                    if f.resolution_notes:\n758\t                        lines.append(f"  回收提示：{f.resolution_notes}")\n759\t                    lines.append("")\n760\t            \n761\t            # 2. 超期伏笔（已过目标回收章节但未回收）\n762\t            if include_overdue:\n763\t                overdue = await self.get_overdue_foreshadows(db, project_id, chapter_number)\n764\t                if overdue:\n765\t                    lines.append("【⚠️ 超期待回收伏笔 - 请尽快回收】")\n766\t                    for f in overdue[:3]:\n767\t                        overdue_chapters = chapter_number - (f.target_resolve_chapter_number or 0)\n768\t                        lines.append(f"- ID:{f.id[:8]} | {f.title} [已超期{overdue_chapters}章]")\n769\t                        lines.append(f"  埋入章节：第{f.plant_chapter_number}章，原计划第{f.target_resolve_chapter_number}章回收")\n770\t                        lines.append(f"  伏笔内容：{f.content[:80]}...")\n771\t                    lines.append("")\n772\t            \n773\t            # 3. 即将需要回收的伏笔（仅作为背景参考，明确禁止提前回收）\n774\t            upcoming_raw = await self.get_pending_resolve_foreshadows(\n775\t                db, project_id, chapter_number, lookahead\n776\t            )\n777\t            # 过滤：排除本章必须回收的和超期的，只保留未来章节的\n778\t            upcoming = [f for f in upcoming_raw\n779\t                       if (f.target_resolve_chapter_number or 0) > chapter_number]\n780\t            \n781\t            if upcoming:\n782\t                lines.append("【📋 近期待回收伏笔（仅供参考，请勿在本章回收）】")\n783\t                lines.append("⚠️ 以下伏笔尚未到回收时机，本章请勿提前回收，仅作为剧情背景了解")\n784\t                for f in upcoming[:5]:\n785\t                    remaining = (f.target_resolve_chapter_number or 0) - chapter_number\n786\t                    lines.append(f"- {f.title}（计划第{f.target_resolve_chapter_number}章回收，还有{remaining}章）")\n787\t                lines.append("")\n788\t            \n789\t            # 4. 本章待埋入伏笔\n790\t            if include_pending:\n791\t                to_plant = await self.get_foreshadows_to_plant(db, project_id, chapter_number)\n792\t                if to_plant:\n793\t                    lines.append("【✨ 本章计划埋入伏笔】")\n794\t                    for f in to_plant:\n795\t                        content_preview = f.content[:80] if len(f.content) > 80 else f.content\n796\t                        lines.append(f"- {f.title}")\n797\t                        lines.append(f"  伏笔内容：{content_preview}")\n798\t                        if f.hint_text:\n799\t                            lines.append(f"  埋入提示：{f.hint_text}")\n800\t                    lines.append("")\n801\t            \n802\t            context_text = "\\n".join(lines) if lines else ""\n803\t            \n804\t            return {\n805\t                "chapter_number": chapter_number,\n806\t                "context_text": context_text,\n807\t                "pending_plant": [f.to_dict() for f in to_plant],\n808\t                "must_resolve": [f.to_dict() for f in must_resolve],\n809\t                "pending_resolve": [f.to_dict() for f in upcoming],\n810\t                "overdue": [f.to_dict() for f in overdue],\n811\t                "recently_planted": []  # 可扩展\n812\t            }\n813\t            \n814\t        except Exception as e:\n815\t            logger.error(f"❌ 构建伏笔上下文失败: {str(e)}")\n816\t            return {\n817\t                "chapter_number": chapter_number,\n818\t                "context_text": "",\n819\t                "pending_plant": [],\n820\t                "must_resolve": [],\n821\t                "pending_resolve": [],\n822\t                "overdue": [],\n823\t                "recently_planted": []\n824\t            }\n825\t    \n826\t    async def get_stats(\n827\t        self,\n828\t        db: AsyncSession,\n829\t        project_id: str,\n830\t        current_chapter: Optional[int] = None\n831\t    ) -> Dict[str, int]:\n832\t        """\n833\t        获取伏笔统计\n834\t        \n835\t        Args:\n836\t            db: 数据库会话\n837\t            project_id: 项目ID\n838\t            current_chapter: 当前章节号(用于计算超期)\n839\t        \n840\t        Returns:\n841\t            统计信息字典\n842\t        """\n843\t        try:\n844\t            # 各状态统计\n845\t            stats_query = (\n846\t                select(\n847\t                    Foreshadow.status,\n848\t                    func.count(Foreshadow.id).label(\'count\')\n849\t                )\n850\t                .where(Foreshadow.project_id == project_id)\n851\t                .group_by(Foreshadow.status)\n852\t            )\n853\t            \n854\t            result = await db.execute(stats_query)\n855\t            status_counts = {row.status: row.count for row in result}\n856\t            \n857\t            # 总数\n858\t            total = sum(status_counts.values())\n859\t            \n860\t            # 长线伏笔数量\n861\t            long_term_query = (\n862\t                select(func.count(Foreshadow.id))\n863\t                .where(\n864\t                    and_(\n865\t                        Foreshadow.project_id == project_id,\n866\t                        Foreshadow.is_long_term == True\n867\t                    )\n868\t                )\n869\t            )\n870\t            long_term_result = await db.execute(long_term_query)\n871\t            long_term_count = long_term_result.scalar() or 0\n872\t            \n873\t            # 超期数量\n874\t            overdue_count = 0\n875\t            if current_chapter:\n876\t                overdue = await self.get_overdue_foreshadows(db, project_id, current_chapter)\n877\t                overdue_count = len(overdue)\n878\t            \n879\t            return {\n880\t                "total": total,\n881\t                "pending": status_counts.get("pending", 0),\n882\t                "planted": status_counts.get("planted", 0),\n883\t                "resolved": status_counts.get("resolved", 0),\n884\t                "partially_resolved": status_counts.get("partially_resolved", 0),\n885\t                "abandoned": status_counts.get("abandoned", 0),\n886\t                "long_term_count": long_term_count,\n887\t                "overdue_count": overdue_count\n888\t            }\n889\t            \n890\t        except Exception as e:\n891\t            logger.error(f"❌ 获取伏笔统计失败: {str(e)}")\n892\t            return {\n893\t                "total": 0,\n894\t                "pending": 0,\n895\t                "planted": 0,\n896\t                "resolved": 0,\n897\t                "partially_resolved": 0,\n898\t                "abandoned": 0,\n899\t                "long_term_count": 0,\n900\t                "overdue_count": 0\n901\t            }\n902\t    \n903\t    async def get_planted_foreshadows_for_analysis(\n904\t        self,\n905\t        db: AsyncSession,\n906\t        project_id: str,\n907\t        current_chapter_number: Optional[int] = None\n908\t    ) -> List[Dict[str, Any]]:\n909\t        """\n910\t        获取用于分析时注入的已埋入伏笔列表（智能过滤版）\n911\t        \n912\t        策略：\n913\t        1. 只返回 status=\'planted\' 的伏笔\n914\t        2. 如果指定了当前章节号，会标记哪些伏笔应该在本章回收\n915\t        3. 区分"可回收"和"不可回收"伏笔，帮助AI正确识别\n916\t        \n917\t        Args:\n918\t            db: 数据库会话\n919\t            project_id: 项目ID\n920\t            current_chapter_number: 当前章节号（可选，用于智能标记）\n921\t        \n922\t        Returns:\n923\t            伏笔列表（带回收标记）\n924\t        """\n925\t        try:\n926\t            query = (\n927\t                select(Foreshadow)\n928\t                .where(\n929\t                    and_(\n930\t                        Foreshadow.project_id == project_id,\n931\t                        Foreshadow.status == "planted"\n932\t                    )\n933\t                )\n934\t                .order_by(Foreshadow.plant_chapter_number)\n935\t            )\n936\t            \n937\t            result = await db.execute(query)\n938\t            foreshadows = result.scalars().all()\n939\t            \n940\t            formatted_list = []\n941\t            for f in foreshadows:\n942\t                item = {\n943\t                    "id": f.id,\n944\t                    "title": f.title,\n945\t                    "content": f.content,\n946\t                    "hint_text": f.hint_text, \n947\t                    "plant_chapter_number": f.plant_chapter_number,\n948\t                    "target_resolve_chapter_number": f.target_resolve_chapter_number,\n949\t                    "category": current_chapter_number:\n957\t                        item["resolve_status"] = "must_resolve_now"  # 本章必须回收\n958\t                        item["resolve_hint"] = "本章必须回收此伏笔"\n959\t                    elif f.target_resolve_chapter_number < current_chapter_number:\n960\t                        item["resolve_status"] = "overdue"  # 已超期\n961\t                        item["resolve_hint"] = f"已超期{current_chapter_number - f.target_resolve_chapter_number}章，应尽快回收"\n962\t                    else:\n963\t                        item["resolve_status"] = "not_yet"  # 尚未到期\n964\t   item["resolve_hint"] = "无明确回收计划，根据剧情自然回收"\n968\t                \n969\t                formatted_list.append(item)\n970\t            \n971\t            return formatted_list\n972\t            \n973\t        except Exception as e:\n974\t            logger.error(f"❌ 获取已埋入伏笔失败: {str(e)}")\n975\t            return []\n976\t    \n977\t    async def delete_chapter_foreshadows(\n978\t        self,\n979\t        db: AsyncSession,\n980\t        project_id: str,\n981\t        chapter_id: str,\n982\t        only_analysis_source: bool = True\n983\t    ) -> Dict[str, Any]:\n984\t        """\n985\t        删除与指定章节相关的伏笔\n986\t        \n987\t        当章节内容被清空或重新生成时调用，清理残留数据\n988\t        \n989\t        Args:\n990\t            db: 数据库会话\n991\t            project_id: 项目ID\n992\t            chapter_id: 章节ID\n993\t            only_analysis_source: 是否只删除来源为 analysis 的伏笔（默认True）\n994\t                                  如果为False，则删除所有与该章节相关的伏笔\n995\t        \n996\t        Returns:\n997\t            删除统计信息\n998\t        """\n999\t        try:\n1000\t            # 1. 先通过 PlotAnalysis 查找该章节的分析ID\n1001\t            # 这是关键：sync_from_analysis 创建的伏笔使用 source_analysis_id 关联\n1002\t            analysis_query = select(PlotAnalysis.id).where(PlotAnalysis.chapter_id == chapter_id)\n1003\t            analysis_result = await db.execute(analysis_query)\n1004\t            analysis_ids = [row[0] for row in analysis_result.fetchall()]\n1005\t            \n1006\t            logger.debug(f"🔍 找到章节 {chapter_id[:8]} 的分析ID: {len(analysis_ids)} 个")\n1007\t            \n1008\t            # 2. 构建查询条件：查找与该章节相关的伏笔\n1009\t            # 匹配方式：\n1010\t            # 1. 埋入章节是该章节 (plant_chapter_id)\n1011\t            # 2. 回收章节是该章节 (actual_resolve_chapter_id)\n1012\t            # 3. 来源分析ID对应该章节的分析 (source_analysis_id)\n1013\t            or_conditions = [\n1014\t                Foreshadow.plant_chapter_id == chapter_id,\n1015\t                Foreshadow.actual_resolve_chapter_id == chapter_id,\n1016\t            ]\n1017\t            \n1018\t            # 如果找到了分析ID，添加 source_analysis_id 匹配条件\n1019\t            if analysis_ids:\n1020\t                or_conditions.append(Foreshadow.source_analysis_id.in_(analysis_ids))\n1021\t            \n1022\t            conditions = [\n1023\t                Foreshadow.project_id == project_id,\n1024\t                or_(*or_conditions)\n1025\t            ]\n1026\t            \n1027\t            # 如果只删除分析来源的伏笔\n1028\t            if only_analysis_source:\n1029\t                conditions.append(Foreshadow.source_type == "analysis")\n1030\t            \n1031\t            # 查询要删除的伏笔\n1032\t            query = select(Foreshadow).where(and_(*conditions))\n1033\t            result = await db.execute(query)\n1034\t            foreshadows_to_delete = result.scalars().all()\n1035\t            \n1036\t            deleted_count = len(foreshadows_to_delete)\n1037\t            deleted_ids = [f.id for f in foreshadows_to_delete]\n1038\t            deleted_titles = [f.title for f in foreshadows_to_delete]\n1039\t            \n1040\t            # 执行删除\n1041\t            for foreshadow in foreshadows_to_delete:\n1042\t                await db.delete(foreshadow)\n1043\t            \n1044\t            await db.commit()\n1045\t            \n1046\t            if deleted_count > 0:\n1047\t                logger.info(f"🗑️ 已删除章节 {chapter_id[:8]} 相关的 {deleted_count} 个伏笔")\n1048\t                for title in deleted_titles[:5]:  # 只打印前5个\n1049\t                    logger.debug(f"  - {title}")\n1050\t                if deleted_count > 5:\n1051\t                    logger.debug(f"  ... 还有 {deleted_count - 5} 个")\n1052\t            \n1053\t            return {\n1054\t                "deleted_count": deleted_count,\n1055\t                "deleted_ids": deleted_ids,\n1056\t                "deleted_titles": deleted_titles\n1057\t            }\n1058\t            \n1059\t        except Exception as e:\n1060\t            await db.rollback()\n1061\t            logger.error(f"❌ 删除章节伏笔失败: {str(e)}")\n1062\t            raise\n1063\t    \n1064\t    async def clean_chapter_analysis_foreshadows(\n1065\t        self,\n1066\t        db: AsyncSession,\n1067\t        project_id: str,\n1068\t        chapter_id: str\n1069\t    ) -> Dict[str, Any]:\n1070\t        """\n1071\t        清理章节分析产生的伏笔（用于重新分析前的清理）\n1072\t        \n1073\t        两步操作：\n1074\t        1. 删除 source_type=\'analysis\' 且 plant_chapter_id == chapter_id 的伏笔\n1075\t        2. 回退在本章被回收的伏笔（将其从 resolved 恢复为 planted）\n1076\t        \n1077\t        保留手动创建的伏笔\n1078\t        \n1079\t        Args:\n1080\t            db: 数据库会话\n1081\t            project_id: 项目ID\n1082\t            chapter_id: 章节ID\n1083\t        \n1084\t        Returns:\n1085\t            清理统计信息\n1086\t        """\n1087\t        try:\n1088\t            # 步骤1: 删除在本章埋入的分析伏笔\n1089\t            query = select(Foreshadow).where(\n1090\t                and_(\n1091\t                    Foreshadow.project_id == project_id,\n1092\t                    Foreshadow.source_type == "analysis",\n1093\t                    Foreshadow.plant_chapter_id == chapter_id\n1094\t                )\n1095\t            )\n1096\t            \n1097\t            result = await db.execute(query)\n1098\t            foreshadows_to_clean = result.scalars().all()\n1099\t            \n1100\t            cleaned_count = len(foreshadows_to_clean)\n1101\t            cleaned_ids = [f.id for f in foreshadows_to_clean]\n1102\t            \n1103\t            for foreshadow in foreshadows_to_clean:\n1104\t                await db.delete(foreshadow)\n1105\t            \n1106\t            # 步骤2: 回退在本章被回收的伏笔（恢复为 planted 状态）\n1107\t            reverted_count = await self._revert_chapter_resolutions(db, project_id, chapter_id)\n1108\t            \n1109\t            await db.commit()\n1110\t            \n1111\t            if cleaned_count > 0 or reverted_count > 0:\n1112\t                logger.info(f"🧹 已清理章节 {chapter_id[:8]}: 删除{cleaned_count}个分析伏笔, 回退{reverted_count}个回收状态")\n1113\t            \n1114\t            return {\n1115\t                "cleaned_count": cleaned_count,\n1116\t                "cleaned_ids": cleaned_ids,\n1117\t                "reverted_count": reverted_count\n1118\t            }\n1119\t            \n1120\t        except Exception as e:\n1121\t            await db.rollback()\n1122\t            logger.error(f"❌ 清理章节分析伏笔失败: {str(e)}")\n1123\t            raise\n1124\t    \n1125\t    async def _revert_chapter_resolutions(\n1126\t        self,\n1127\t        db: AsyncSession,\n1128\t        project_id: str,\n1129\t        chapter_id: str\n1130\t    ) -> int:\n1131\t        """\n1132\t        回退在指定章节中被回收的伏笔\n1133\t        \n1134\t        将 actual_resolve_chapter_id == chapter_id 且 status 为 resolved/partially_resolved 的伏笔\n1135\t        恢复为 planted 状态，以便重新分析时可以重新匹配回收\n1136\t        \n1137\t        Args:\n1138\t            db: 数据库会话\n1139\t            project_id: 项目ID\n1140\t            chapter_id: 章节ID\n1141\t        \n1142\t        Returns:\n1143\t            回退的伏笔数量\n1144\t        """\n1145\t        try:\n1146\t            update_query = (\n1147\t                update(Foreshadow)\n1148\t                .where(\n1149\t                    and_(\n1150\t                        Foreshadow.project_id == project_id,\n1151\t                        Foreshadow.actual_resolve_chapter_id == chapter_id,\n1152\t                        Foreshadow.status.in_(["resolved", "partially_resolved"])\n1153\t                    )\n1154\t                )\n1155\t                .values(\n1156\t                    status="planted",\n1157\t                    actual_resolve_chapter_id=None,\n1158\t                    actual_resolve_chapter_number=None,\n1159\t                    resolved_at=None,\n1160\t                    resolution_text=None\n1161\t                )\n1162\t            )\n1163\t            result = await db.execute(update_query)\n1164\t            reverted_count = result.rowcount\n1165\t            \n1166\t            if reverted_count > 0:\n1167\t                logger.info(f"↩️ 回退了 {reverted_count} 个在章节 {chapter_id[:8]} 中被回收的伏笔")\n1168\t            \n1169\t            return reverted_count\n1170\t            \n1171\t        except Exception as e:\n1172\t            logger.error(f"❌ 回退章节回收失败: {str(e)}")\n1173\t            return 0\n1174\t\n1175\t    async def clear_project_foreshadows_for_reset(\n1176\t        self,\n1177\t        db: AsyncSession,\n1178\t        project_id: str\n1179\t    ) -> Dict[str, int]:\n1180\t        """\n1181\t        全新生成时清理项目伏笔\n1182\t        \n1183\t        1. 删除所有 source_type=\'analysis\' 的伏笔\n1184\t        2. 重置所有 source_type=\'manual\' 的伏笔为 pending 状态\n1185\t        \n1186\t        Args:\n1187\t            db: 数据库会话\n1188\t            project_id: 项目ID\n1189\t            \n1190\t        Returns:\n1191\t            清理统计\n1192\t        """\n1193\t        try:\n1194\t            # 1. 删除分析产生的伏笔\n1195\t            delete_query = delete(Foreshadow).where(\n1196\t                and_(\n1197\t                    Foreshadow.project_id == project_id,\n1198\t                    Foreshadow.source_type == "analysis"\n1199\t                )\n1200\t            )\n1201\t            delete_result = await db.execute(delete_query)\n1202\t            deleted_count = delete_result.rowcount\n1203\t            \n1204\t            # 2. 重置手动创建的伏笔\n1205\t            # 将 planted/resolved/partially_resolved 状态重置为 pending\n1206\t            # 清空章节关联信息\n1207\t            update_query = (\n1208\t                update(Foreshadow)\n1209\t                .where(\n1210\t                    and_(\n1211\t                        Foreshadow.project_id == project_id,\n1212\t                        Foreshadow.source_type == "manual",\n1213\t                        Foreshadow.status.in_(["planted", "resolved", "partially_resolved"])\n1214\t                    )\n1215\t                )\n1216\t                .values(\n1217\t                    status="pending",\n1218\t                    plant_chapter_id=None,\n1219\t                    plant_chapter_number=None,\n1220\t                    actual_resolve_chapter_id=None,\n1221\t                    actual_resolve_chapter_number=None,\n1222\t                    planted_at=None,\n1223\t                    resolved_at=None,\n1224\t                    target_resolve_chapter_id=None,\n1225\t                    target_resolve_chapter_number=None\n1226\t                )\n1227\t            )\n1228\t            update_result = await db.execute(update_query)\n1229\t            reset_count = update_result.rowcount\n1230\t            \n1231\t            await db.commit()\n1232\t            \n1233\t            logger.info(f"🧹 项目 {project_id} 伏笔清理完成: 删除 {deleted_count} 个分析伏笔, 重置 {reset_count} 个手动伏笔")\n1234\t            \n1235\t            return {\n1236\t                "deleted_count": deleted_count,\n1237\t                "reset_count": reset_count\n1238\t            }\n1239\t            \n1240\t        except Exception as e:\n1241\t            await db.rollback()\n1242\t            logger.error(f"❌ 清理项目伏笔失败: {str(e)}")\n1243\t            raise\n1244\t\n1245\t    async def auto_update_from_analysis(\n1246\t        self,\n1247\t        db: AsyncSession,\n1248\t        project_id: str,\n1249\t        chapter_id: str,\n1250\t        chapter_number: int,\n1251\t        analysis_foreshadows: List[Dict[str, Any]]\n1252\t    ) -> Dict[str, Any]:\n1253\t        """\n1254\t        根据章节分析结果自动更新伏笔状态\n1255\t        \n1256\t        功能：\n1257\t        1. 自动标记新埋入的伏笔为 planted\n1258\t        2. 根据 reference_foreshadow_id 自动回收已有伏笔\n1259\t        3. 如果没有 reference_foreshadow_id，使用内容匹配备用机制\n1260\t        4. 创建新发现的伏笔记录\n1261\t        \n1262\t        Args:\n1263\t            db: 数据库会话\n1264\t            project_id: 项目ID\n1265\t            chapter_id: 章节ID\n1266\t            chapter_number: 章节号\n1267\t            analysis_foreshadows: 分析结果中的伏笔列表\n1268\t        \n1269\t        Returns:\n1270\t            更新统计\n1271\t        """\n1272\t        try:\n1273\t            stats = {\n1274\t                "planted_count": 0,      # 新埋入的伏笔\n1275\t                "resolved_count": 0,     # 回收的伏笔\n1276\t                "created_count": 0,      # 新创建的伏笔记录\n1277\t                "updated_ids": [],       # 更新的伏笔ID\n1278\t                "created_ids": [],       # 创建的伏笔ID\n1279\t                "matched_by_content": 0, # 通过内容匹配回收的数量\n1280\t                "errors": []             # 错误信息\n1281\t            }\n1282\t            \n1283\t            # 预先获取所有已埋入的伏笔，用于内容匹配\n1284\t            planted_foreshadows = await self.get_planted_foreshadows_for_analysis(db, project_id)\n1285\t            \n1286\t            for fs_data in analysis_foreshadows:\n1287\t                try:\n1288\t                    fs_type = fs_data.get("type", "planted")\n1289\t                    reference_id = fs_data.get("reference_foreshadow_id")\n1290\t                    \n1291\t                    if fs_type == "resolved":\n1292\t                        existing = None\n1293\t                        matched_by_content = False\n1294\t                        \n1295\t                        # 策略1: 优先使用 reference_id 精确匹配\n1296\t                        # 重要：如果分析结果里已经给出了 reference_foreshadow_id，\n1297\t                        # 但该伏笔已被用户删除或已不属于当前项目，则直接跳过，\n1298\t                        # 不再退回内容匹配，避免把“已删除伏笔”的旧分析结果错误同步到其他同名/近似伏笔上。\n1299\t                        if reference_id:\n1300\t                            existing = await self.get_foreshadow(db, reference_id)\n1301\t                            if existing and existing.project_id == project_id:\n1302\t                                logger.info(f"🎯 通过ID精确匹配伏笔: {existing.title}")\n1303\t                            else:\n1304\t                                existing = None\n1305\t                                logger.warning(f"⚠️ 伏笔ID不存在或不属于该项目，跳过本次回收同步: {reference_id}")\n1306\t                                stats["skipped_resolve_count"] = stats.get("skipped_resolve_count", 0) + 1\n1307\t                                stats["errors"].append(f"reference_foreshadow_id 无效或已删除: {reference_id}")\n1308\t                                continue\n1309\t                        \n1310\t                        # 策略2: 内容匹配备用机制（仅在 analysis 未提供 reference_id 时启用）\n1311\t                        if not reference_id and not existing and planted_foreshadows:\n1312\t                            matched = self._match_foreshadow_by_content(\n1313\t                                fs_data, planted_foreshadows\n1314\t                            )\n1315\t                            if matched:\n1316\t                                matched_by_content = True\n1317\t                                logger.info(f"🔍 通过内容匹配找到伏笔: {matched.get(\'title\')}")\n1318\t                                # 重新获取完整的伏笔对象\n1319\t                                existing = await self.get_foreshadow(db, matched.get(\'id\'))\n1320\t                        \n1321\t                        # 检查伏笔是否已被回收（防止重复回收）\n1322\t                        if existing:\n1323\t                            if existing.status == "resolved" and existing.actual_resolve_chapter_number == chapter_number:\n1324\t                                logger.info(f"ℹ️ 伏笔已在本章回收过，跳过: {existing.title}")\n1325\t                                continue\n1326\t                            elif existing.status == "resolved":\n1327\t                                logger.warning(f"⚠️ 伏笔已在第{existing.actual_resolve_chapter_number}章回收，跳过: {existing.title}")\n1328\t                                continue\n1329\t                        \n1330\t                        # 执行回收\n1331\t                        if existing and existing.status == "planted":\n1332\t                            # 更新为已回收状态\n1333\t                            existing.status = "resolved"\n1334\t                            existing.actual_resolve_chapter_id = chapter_id\n1335\t                            existing.actual_resolve_chapter_number = chapter_number\n1336\t                            existing.resolved_at = datetime.now()\n1337\t                            \n1338\t                            # 更新回收文本\n1339\t                            if fs_data.get("content"):\n1340\t                                existing.resolution_text = fs_data.get("content")\n1341\t                            \n1342\t                            await db.flush()\n1343\t                            await db.refresh(existing)\n1344\t                            \n1345\t                            stats["resolved_count"] += 1\n1346\t                            stats["updated_ids"].append(existing.id)\n1347\t                            if matched_by_content:\n1348\t                                stats["matched_by_content"] += 1\n1349\t                            logger.info(f"✅ 自动回收伏笔: {existing.title} (ID: {existing.id}, status: {existing.status})")\n1350\t                            \n1351\t                            # 从待匹配列表中移除已回收的伏笔\n1352\t                            planted_foreshadows = [f for f in planted_foreshadows if f[\'id\'] != existing.id]\n1353\t                        elif existing:\n1354\t                            logger.warning(f"⚠️ 伏笔状态不是planted，跳过回收: {existing.title} (status: {existing.status})")\n1355\t                        else:\n1356\t                            # 找不到匹配的已埋入伏笔，跳过（不创建新记录！）\n1357\t                            # 核心原则：只有"埋入"操作会创建伏笔记录，"回收"只是更新已有记录\n1358\t                            # 如果没有埋入的伏笔，就不可能存在回收\n1359\t                            fs_title = fs_data.get("title", fs_data.get("content", "")[:30])\n1360\t                            logger.warning(f"⚠️ 未找到匹配的已埋入伏笔，跳过回收（不创建新记录）: {fs_title}")\n1361\t                            logger.warning(f"   提示：AI可能误识别了回收伏笔，或者 reference_foreshadow_id 未正确填写")\n1362\t                            stats["skipped_resolve_count"] = stats.get("skipped_resolve_count", 0) + 1\n1363\t                            continue\n1364\t                    \n1365\t                    elif fs_type == 伏笔内容为空，跳过")\n1369\t                            continue\n1370\t                        \n1371\t                        fs_title = fs_data.get("title", "")\n1372\t                        if not chapter_id + content_hash）\n1376\t                        source_memory_id = generate_stable_foreshadow_id(\n1377\t                            chapter_id, fs_content, fs_type\n1378\t                        )\n1379\t                        \n1380\t                        # 检查是否已存在（使用稳定ID去重，防止重复分析创建重复记录）\n1381\t                        existing_check = await db.execute(\n1382\t                            select(Foreshadow).where(\n1383\t                                and_(\n1384\t                                    Foreshadow.project_id == project_id,\n1385\t                                    or_(\n1386\t                                        # 方式1：通过稳定source_memory_id精确匹配\n1387\t                                        Foreshadow.source_memory_id == source_memory_id,\n1388\t                                        # 方式2：通过标题+章节号匹配（兼容旧数据）\n1389\t                                        and_(\n1390\t                                            Foreshadow.title == fs_title,\n1391\t                                            Foreshadow.plant_chapter_id == chapter_id,\n1392\t                                            Foreshadow.source_type == "analysis"\n1393\t                                        )\n1394\t                                    )\n1395\t                                )\n1396\t                            )\n1397\t                        )\n1398\t                        existing_fs = existing_check.scalar_one_or_none()\n1399\t                        \n1400\t                        if existing_fs:\n1401\t                            # 更新已存在的伏笔，避免重复创建\n1402\t                            existing_fs.title = fs_title\n1403\t                            existing_fs.content = fs_content\n1404\t                            existing_fs.strength = fs_data.get("strength", existing_fs.strength)\n1405\t                            existing_fs.subtlety = fs_data.get("subtlety", existing_fs.subtlety)\n1406\t                            existing_fs.hint_text = fs_data.get("keyword", existing_fs.hint_text)\n1407\t                            existing_fs.category = fs_data.get("category", existing_fs.category)\n1408\t                            existing_fs.is_long_term = fs_data.get("is_long_term", existing_fs.is_long_term)\n1409\t                            existing_fs.related_characters = fs_data.get("related_characters", existing_fs.related_characters)\n1410\t                            if fs_data.get("estimated_resolve_chapter"):\n1411\t                                existing_fs.target_resolve_chapter_number = fs_data.get("estimated_resolve_chapter")\n1412\t                            # 更新为稳定的source_memory_id\n1413\t                            existing_fs.source_memory_id = source_memory_id\n1414\t                            await db.flush()\n1415\t                            stats["updated_ids"].append(existing_fs.id)\n1416\t                            logger.info(f"📝 更新已存在伏笔（避免重复）: {fs_title} (ID: {existing_fs.id})")\n1417\t                        else:\n1418\t                            # 创建新伏笔\n1419\t                            # 不再为 estimated_resolve_chapter 设置默认值，避免误报"超期"\n1420\t                            estimated_resolve = fs_data.get("estimated_resolve_chapter")\n1421\t                            if estimated_resolve is None:\n1422\t                                logger.info(f"ℹ️ AI未填写estimated_resolve_chapter，不设默认值，标记为无明确回收计划")\n1423\t                            \n1424\t                            new_foreshadow = Foreshadow(\n1425\t content=fs_content,\n1429\t                                hint_text=fs_data.get("keyword"),\n1430\t                                source_type="analysis",\n1431\t 通过内容相似度匹配伏笔（备用机制）\n1546\t        \n1547\t        匹配策略（按优先级）：\n1548\t        1. 标题完全匹配（权重最高）\n1549\t        2. 标题部分匹配（包含关系）\n1550\t        3. 标题关键词匹配（去除"回收"等后缀）\n1551\t        4. 关键词匹配\n1552\t              score = 1.0\n1596\t                    logger.debug(f"🎯 标题完全匹配: \'{resolved_title}\' == \'{fs_title}\'")\n1597\t                elif resolved_title_clean and resolved_title_clean == 0.15  # 加分\n1626\t            \n1627\t            # 策略5: 分类匹配\n1628\t            if resolved_category and fs_category:\n1629\t                if resolved_category == fs_category:\n1630\t _calculate_word_overlap(self, text1: str, text2: str) -> float:\n1648\t        """\n1649\t        计算两个文本的词重叠度\n1650\t        \n1651\t        使用字符级别的 n-gram 相似度计算\n1652\t        \n1653\t        Args:\n1654\t            text1: 文本1\n1655\t            text2: 文本2\n1656\t        \n1657\t        Returns:\n1658\t            0-1之间的相似度分数\n1659\t        """\n1660\t        if not text1 or not "").replace("\\n", "")\n1666\t            if len(text) < n:\n1667\t                return {text}\n1668\t            return {text[i:i+n] for i in range(len(text) - n + 1)}\n1669\t        \n1670\t \n199\t        # 初始化上下文\n200\t        context = OneToManyContext(\n201\t            chapter_number=chapter_number,\n202\t            chapter_title=chapter.title or "",\n203\t """构建1-N模式的角色信息（完整版：含年龄、外貌、背景、关系、组织、职业）+ 独立职业详情"""\n317\t        from sqlalchemy import or_\n318\t        \n319\t        # 获取所有角色\n320\t        characters_result = await db.execute(\n321\t 从expansion_plan中提取角色焦点\n332\t        filter_character_names = None\n333\t        if chapter.expansion_plan:\n334\t            try:\n335\t                plan = CharacterRelationship.character_from_id.in_(character_ids),\n358\t                    CharacterRelationship.character_to_id.in_(character_ids)\n359\t                )\n360\t            )\n361\t        )\n362\t        all_rels = rels_result.scalars().all()\n363\t        \n364\t        # 按角色ID分组关系\n365\t        char_rels_map: Dict[str, List] = {cid: [] for cid in character_ids}\n366\t        for r in  db: AsyncSession\n586\t    ) -> Optional[str]:\n587\t        """构建最近10章的expansion_plan摘要"""\n588\t        try:\n589\t            result = await db.execute(\n590\t                select(Chapter.chapter_number, Chapter.title, Chapter.expansion_plan, Chapter.summary)\n591\t                .where(Chapter.project_id == project_id)\n592\t                .where(Chapter.chapter_number < chapter.chapter_number)\n593\t                .order_by(Chapter.chapter_number.desc())\n594\t                .limit(self.RECENT_CHAPTERS_COUNT)\n595\t            )\n596\t            recent_chapters = result.all()\n597\t            \n598\t            if not recent_chapters:\n599\t                return None\n600\t            \n601\t            # 按章节号正序排列\n602\t            recent_chapters = sorted(recent_chapters, key=lambda x: x[0])\n603\t            \n604\t            lines = ["【最近章节规划】"]\n605\t            for ch_num, ch_title, expansion_plan, summary in recent_chapters:\n606\t                if expansion_plan:\n607\t                    try:\n608\t                        plan = json.loads(expansion_plan)\n609\t                        plot_summary = plan.get(\'plot_summary\', \'\')\n610\t                        key_events = plan.get(\'key_events\', [])\n611\t                        events_str = \'；\'.join(key_events[:3]) if key_events else \'\'\n612\t                        line = f"第{ch_num}章《{ch_title}》：{plot_summary}"\n613\t                        if events_str:\n614\t                            line += f"（关键事件：{events_str}）"\n615\t                        lines.append(line)\n616\t                    except json.JSONDecodeError:\n617\t                        if summary:\n618\t                            lines.append(f"第{ch_num}章《{ch_title}》：{summary[:100]}")\n619\t                elif summary:\n620\t                    lines.append(f"第{ch_num}章《{ch_title}》：{summary[:100]}")\n621\t            \n622\t            if len(lines) <= 1:\n623\t                return None\n624\t            \n625\t            return "\\n".join(lines)\n626\t        except Exception as e:\n627\t            logger.error(f"❌ str,\n634\t        chapter_number: int,\n635\t        chapter_outline: str,\n636\t        db: AsyncSession\n637\t    ) -> Optional[str]:\n638\t        """获取相关记忆（始终启用，相关度>0.6）"""\n639\t        if not {str(e)}")\n672\t            return None\n673\t    \n674\t    async def _get_last_ending_enhanced(\n675\t        self,\n676\t        chapter: Chapter,\n677\t        db: AsyncSession,\n678\t \n780\t    async def _get_relevant_memories(\n781\t        self,\n782\t        user_id: str,\n783\t        project_id: str,\n784\t        chapter_number: int,\n785\t        chapter_outline: str,\n786\t        limit: int = 3\n787\t    ) -> Optional[str]:\n788\t        """\n789\t        获取与本章最相关的记忆\n790\t        \n791\t        注意：伏笔相关信息统一由 _get_foreshadow_reminders() 通过 foreshadow_service 提供，\n792\t        此方法只负责获取故事记忆，不再从旧的 memory_service 获取伏笔信息。\n793\t        """\n794\t        if not self.memory_service:\n795\t            return None\n796\t        \n797\t        try:\n798\t      limit=limit,\n803\t                min_importance=self.MEMORY_IMPORTANCE_THRESHOLD\n804\t            )\n805\t            \n806\t            return self._format_memories(relevant, _format_memories(\n813\t        self,\n814\t        relevant: List[Dict[str, Any]],\n815\t        max_length: int = 500\n816\t    ) -> str:\n817\t        """格式化记忆为简洁文本（纯记忆，不含伏笔）"""\n818\t        if not relevant:\n819\t            return None\n820\t        \n821\t        lines = ["【相关记忆】"]\n822\t        current_length = 0\n823\t        \n824\t        for mem in relevant:\n825\t            content = mem.get(\'content\', \'\')[:80]\n826\t            text = f"- {content}"\n827\t            if current_length + len(text) > max_length:\n828\t                break\n829\t            lines.append(text)\n830\t            current_length += len(text)\n831\t        \n832\t        return "\\n".join(lines) if len(lines) > 1 else None\n833\t    \n834\t    async def _get_foreshadow_reminders(\n835\t        self,\n836\t        project_id: str,\n837\t        chapter_number: int,\n838\t        db: AsyncSession\n839\t    ) -> Optional[str]:\n840\t        """\n841\t        获取伏笔提醒信息（增强版）\n842\t        \n843\t        策略：\n844\t        1. 本章必须回收的伏笔（target_resolve_chapter_number == chapter_number）\n845\t        2. 超期未回收的伏笔（target_resolve_chapter_number < chapter_number）\n846\t        3. 即将到期的伏笔（target_resolve_chapter_number 在未来3章内）\n847\t        """\n848\t        if not self.foreshadow_service:\n849\t            return None\n850\t        \n851\t        try:\n852\t            lines = []\n853\t            \n854\t            # 1. 本章必须回收的伏笔\n855\t            must_resolve = await self.foreshadow_service.get_must_resolve_foreshadows(\n856\t                db=db,\n857\t                project_id=project_id,\n858\t                chapter_number=chapter_number\n859\t            )\n860\t            \n861\t            if must_resolve:\n862\t                lines.append("【🎯 本章必须回收的伏笔】")\n863\t                for f in must_resolve:\n864\t                    lines.append(f"- {f.title}")\n865\t                    lines.append(f"  埋入章节：第{f.plant_chapter_number}章")\n866\t                    lines.append(f"  伏笔内容：{f.content[:100]}{\'...\' if len(f.content) > 100 else \'\'}")\n867\t                    if f.resolution_notes:\n868\t                        lines.append(f"  回收提示：{f.resolution_notes}")\n869\t                    lines.append("")\n870\t            \n871\t            # 2. 超期未回收的伏笔\n872\t            overdue = await self.foreshadow_service.get_overdue_foreshadows(\n873\t                db=db,\n874\t                project_id=project_id,\n875\t                current_chapter=chapter_number\n876\t            )\n877\t            \n878\t            if overdue:\n879\t                lines.append("【⚠️ 超期待回收伏笔】")\n880\t                for f in overdue[:3]:  # 最多显示3个\n881\t                    overdue_chapters = chapter_number - (f.target_resolve_chapter_number or 0)\n882\t                    lines.append(f"- {f.title} [已超期{overdue_chapters}章]")\n883\t                    lines.append(f"  埋入章节：第{f.plant_chapter_number}章，原计划第{f.target_resolve_chapter_number}章回收")\n884\t                    lines.append(f"  伏笔内容：{f.content[:80]}...")\n885\t                    lines.append("")\n886\t            \n887\t            # 3. 即将到期的伏笔（未来3章内）\n888\t            upcoming = await self.foreshadow_service.get_pending_resolve_foreshadows(\n889\t                db=db,\n890\t                project_id=project_id,\n891\t                current_chapter=chapter_number,\n892\t                lookahead=3\n893\t            )\n894\t            \n895\t            # 过滤：只保留未来章节的，排除本章和超期的\n896\t            upcoming_filtered = [f for f in upcoming\n897\t                               if (f.target_resolve_chapter_number or 0) > chapter_number]\n898\t            \n899\t            if upcoming_filtered:\n900\t                lines.append("【📋 即将到期的伏笔（仅供参考）】")\n901\t                for f in upcoming_filtered[:3]:  # 最多显示3个\n902\t                    remaining = (f.target_resolve_chapter_number or 0) - chapter_number\n903\t                    lines.append(f"- {f.title}（计划第{f.target_resolve_chapter_number}章回收，还有{remaining}章）")\n904\t                lines.append("")\n905\t            \n906\t            return "\\n".join(lines) if lines else None\n907\t            \n908\t        except Exception as e:\n909\t            logger.error(f"❌ 获取伏笔提醒失败: {str(e)}")\n910\t            return None\n911\t    \n912\t    async def _build_story_skeleton(\n913\t        self,\n914\t        project_id: str,\n915\t        chapter_number: int,\n916\t        db: AsyncSession\n917\t    ) -> Optional[str]:\n918\t        """构建故事骨架（每N章采样）"""\n919\t        try:\n920\t            result = await db.execute(\n921\t                select(Chapter.id, OneToOneContextBuilder:\n963\t    """\n964\t    1-1模式上下文构建器\n965\t    \n966\t    上下文构建策略：\n967\t    P0核心信息：\n968\t    1. 从outline.structure的JSON中提取：summary, scenes, key_points, emotion, goal\n969\t Args:\n985\t            memory_service: 记忆服务实例（可选）\n986\t            foreshadow_service: 伏笔服务实例（可选）\n987\t        """\n988\t        self.memory_service = memory_service\n989\t        self.foreshadow_service = foreshadow_service\n990\t    \n991\t    async def build(\n992\t        self,\n993\t        chapter: Chapter,\n994\t        project: Project,\n995\t        outline: 构建1-1模式上下文\n1002\t        \n1003\t        Args:\n1004\t            chapter: 章节对象\n1005\t            project: 项目对象\n1006\t            outline: 大纲对象\n1007\t            user_id: 用户ID\n1008\t       if len(content) <= 500:\n1050\t                    context.continuation_point = content\n1051\t                else:\n1052\t                    context.continuation_point =            summary_result = await db.execute(\n1057\t                    select(StoryMemory.content)\n1058\t                    .where(StoryMemory.project_id == chapter.project_id)\n1059\t )\n1063\t                summary_mem = summary_result.scalar_one_or_none()\n1064\t                \n1065\t                if summary_mem:\n1066\t                    context.previous_chapter_summary = 根据structure中的characters获取角色信息（含职业）\n1084\t        character_names = []\n1085\t        if outline and outline.structure:\n1086\t            try:\n1087\t                structure = .where(Character.name.in_(character_names))\n1104\t            )\n1105\t            characters = characters_result.scalars().all()\n1106\t            \n1107\t            if characters:\n1108\t {len(context.chapter_characters)}字符")\n1118\t                logger.info(f"  ✅ P1-职业信息: {len(context.chapter_careers or \'\')}字符")\n1119\t            else:\n1120\t **[] 用户：**

我知道怎么优化我们的skills了，我下载两个开源ai写作软件你看看源代码，临时\MuMuAINovel和临时\MuMuAINovel，你看看总有我们没有的，我感觉可以使用gsd或者superpower


---

**[2026-04-19 09:04:45] AI 回复：**

读完了核心代码。MuMuAINovel 是一个完整的 Web 应用（Python 后端 + Vue 前端 + 数据库），功能远超我们的 skill 体系。以下是**我们真正能借鉴的东西**：

---

## MuMuAINovel 核心功能 vs 我们现有的

| MuMuAINovel 功能 | 实现方式 | 我们有什么 | 差距 |
|---|---|---|---|
| **RTCO 分层上下文构建** | P0核心/P1重要/P2参考 | 读所有文件无优先级 | 大 |
| **智能伏笔管理** | 状态机(pending→planted→resolved)+超期检测+自动匹配 | `pending_hooks.md` 简单列表 | 巨大 |
| **AI 章节分析** | 自动提取钩子/伏笔/冲突/角色状态/评分 | `chapter_health_check.py` 只查AI率 | 大 |
| **角色状态自动追踪** | 心理状态+亲密度数值+组织归属+死亡/退场级联 | `character_relationships.md` 手动更新 | 大 |
| **向量记忆搜索** | 语义检索相关章节记忆 | 无 | 需要数据库，暂不可行 |
| **提示词工坊** | 用户可自定义各类提示词模板 | 无 | 中 |
| **职业/阶级体系** | 角色职业+阶段+升级 | `power_tracking.md` 简单追踪 | 小 |

## 值得且能借鉴到 skill 的功能（按优先级）

### 1. RTCO 分层上下文（高优先，立即可做）

MuMuAINovel 在生成每章时构建**结构化上下文**，分三层优先级：

```
P0 核心（每次必送）：
  - 本章大纲/任务要求
  - 前1章最后500字（衔接锚点）
  - 前1章剧情摘要
  
P1 重要（通常送）：
  - 本章涉及角色的完整信息（含关系、状态）
  - 情感基调
  - 伏笔提醒
  
P2 参考（按需送）：
  - 历史章节摘要
  - 远期伏笔状态
```

**我们现在的问题**：步骤一只说"读状态卡和 task_plan"，没有规定**上下文的优先级和结构**，模型可能塞太多无用信息或漏掉关键信息。

### 2. 智能伏笔管理（高优先，可用 markdown 模拟）

MuMuAINovel 的伏笔系统有**状态机**：
- `pending` → `planted`(已埋入) → `resolved`(已回收)
- 自动检测**超期伏笔**（计划第10章回收但已经写到第15章了）
- 自动检测**必须回收**（计划本章回收的伏笔）
- 生成时**自动注入**伏笔提醒到上下文

**我们现在**：`pending_hooks.md` 只是简单列表，没有状态追踪和超期检测。

### 3. AI 章节分析（中优先，可扩展脚本）

MuMuAINovel 每章写完自动用 AI 分析：
- 钩子类型和强度
- 伏笔埋入/回收
- 冲突等级和进度
- 角色心理状态变化
- 整体评分（节奏/吸引力/连贯性）

**我们现在**：`chapter_health_check.py` 只做统计指标，不分析内容质量。

### 4. 角色状态自动追踪（中优先，可扩展文件格式）

MuMuAINovel 追踪：
- 心理状态（如"自信→谨慎"）
- 亲密度数值（-100到100，自动调整）
- 存活状态（active/deceased/missing/retired）
- 组织归属变化

**我们现在**：`character_relationships.md` 全靠手动更新。

---

## 建议方案

你想用 gsd 或 superpower 来做这个优化。我的建议：

**把 RTCO 分层上下文 + 智能伏笔管理** 写入 skill，这两个是改善写作质量最关键的。

要不要我现在开始实施？还是你想先看看第二个开源项目？
